kompiuteris","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Dominoes is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9MT6DZHGLM46","TileLayout":"Poster","Title":"Soccer Penalty 2018","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.19098.13818451027377821.478bfd2d-8f08-4373-a427-444cdec8e647.3a7f4de2-34bd-4135-82bf-517f7338a646","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.11099.13818451027377821.478bfd2d-8f08-4373-a427-444cdec8e647.471a7255-5cb1-4ccc-8d11-d5ac9bdac9c9","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Nemokama","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["41633NinjaBlitzWarGames.SoccerPenalty2018_qnq5anfshaxke"],"ContentIds":["ddc1be56-bcc3-e8ec-79cf-18dcdaaa7dba","4975852c-8ac9-ab37-a096-784902a42501"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"Asmeninis kompiuteris","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Are you good at football? Be birželis 1968 leidime Scientific American Martin Gardner skiltyje aprašytos jo \"matematinių žaidimų\" žaidimą Cl Baker, kuri yra panaši į FreeCell, išskyrus korteles Tableau yra pastatytas kostiumas, o ne alternatyvių spalvų. Gardneris rašė: \"Žaidimas buvo mokomi Baker jo tėvas, kuris, savo ruožtu, išmoko jį iš anglas per 1920\". Šis variantas yra dabar vadinamas Kepimo Žaidimas. FreeCell ištakos gali datuojamas dar 1945 ir Skandinavijos žaidimas vadinamas Napoleono Sankt Helena (ne žaidimo Napoleono Šv Helena, taip pat žinomas kaip keturiasdešimt Thieves).\r\n\r\nPaulius Alfille pasikeitė Baker rungtynes ​​darant kortelės statyti pagal pakaitinių spalvos, tokiu būdu sukuriant FreeCell. Jis įgyvendino pirmąjį kompiuterinį variantą jį Kuratorius programavimo kalba PLATO švietimo kompiuterinės sistemos 1978 Alfille galėjo rodyti lengvai atpažįstami grafinius vaizdus žaisti kortas ant 512 * 512 nespalvoto ekrano ant PLATO sistemas.\r\n\r\nŠis originalus FreeCell aplinka leido žaidimus su 4C10 1C10 kolonų ir ląstelių Be standartinio 8 * 4 žaidimą. Kiekvienam variantui, programa saugomi eiliškumo sąrašą su ilgiausių laimi dryželiais žaidėjų. Taip pat buvo turnyras sistema, kuri leido žmonėms konkuruoti laimėti sunkias rankų pakėlė pasiūlymus. Paulius Alfille apibūdina šį ankstyvą Freecell aplinką išsamiau interviu nuo 2000.\r\n\r\n\r\nSprendėjas sudėtingumas\r\nFreeCell žaidimas turi pastovų skaičių korteles.
